          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: space-between;
          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: nowrap;
          box-sizing: border-box;
          padding-top: 0.5em;
        }
        .container-outside {
          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        <p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





Lenovo ThinkPad C13 Yoga Chromebook is using amd graphics card, the driver is amd drm gpu driver. The zork board's latest kernel version is 5.4.



<span class="line"><!---->Lenovo ThinkPad C13 Yoga Chromebook is using amd graphics card, the driver is amd drm gpu driver. The zork board's latest kernel version is 5.4.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In function amdgpu_gem_va_ioctl, there are two integer overflow in sub functions amdgpu_vm_bo_map and amdgpu_vm_bo_replace_map.



<span class="line"><!---->In function amdgpu_gem_va_ioctl, there are two integer overflow in sub functions amdgpu_vm_bo_map and amdgpu_vm_bo_replace_map.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





int amdgpu_gem_va_ioctl(struct drm_device *dev, void *data,



<span class="line"><!---->int amdgpu_gem_va_ioctl(struct drm_device *dev, void *data,<!----></span>



<br>





			  struct drm_file *filp)



<span class="line"><!---->			  struct drm_file *filp)<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>





//skip..



<span class="line"><!---->//skip..<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	switch (args->operation) {



<span class="line"><!---->	switch (args-&gt;operation) {<!----></span>



<br>





	case AMDGPU_VA_OP_MAP:



<span class="line"><!---->	case AMDGPU_VA_OP_MAP:<!----></span>



<br>





		va_flags = amdgpu_gmc_get_pte_flags(adev, args->flags);



<span class="line"><!---->		va_flags = amdgpu_gmc_get_pte_flags(adev, args-&gt;flags);<!----></span>



<br>





		r = amdgpu_vm_bo_map(adev, bo_va, args->va_address,



<span class="line"><!---->		r = amdgpu_vm_bo_map(adev, bo_va, args-&gt;va_address,<!----></span>



<br>





				     args->offset_in_bo, args->map_size,  <------



<span class="line"><!---->				     args-&gt;offset_in_bo, args-&gt;map_size,  &lt;------<!----></span>



<br>





				     va_flags);



<span class="line"><!---->				     va_flags);<!----></span>



<br>





		break;



<span class="line"><!---->		break;<!----></span>



<br>





	case AMDGPU_VA_OP_UNMAP:



<span class="line"><!---->	case AMDGPU_VA_OP_UNMAP:<!----></span>



<br>





		r = amdgpu_vm_bo_unmap(adev, bo_va, args->va_address);



<span class="line"><!---->		r = amdgpu_vm_bo_unmap(adev, bo_va, args-&gt;va_address);<!----></span>



<br>





		break;



<span class="line"><!---->		break;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	case AMDGPU_VA_OP_CLEAR:



<span class="line"><!---->	case AMDGPU_VA_OP_CLEAR:<!----></span>



<br>





		r = amdgpu_vm_bo_clear_mappings(adev, &fpriv->vm,



<span class="line"><!---->		r = amdgpu_vm_bo_clear_mappings(adev, &amp;fpriv-&gt;vm,<!----></span>



<br>





						args->va_address,



<span class="line"><!---->						args-&gt;va_address,<!----></span>



<br>





						args->map_size);



<span class="line"><!---->						args-&gt;map_size);<!----></span>



<br>





		break;



<span class="line"><!---->		break;<!----></span>



<br>





	case AMDGPU_VA_OP_REPLACE:



<span class="line"><!---->	case AMDGPU_VA_OP_REPLACE:<!----></span>



<br>





		va_flags = amdgpu_gmc_get_pte_flags(adev, args->flags);



<span class="line"><!---->		va_flags = amdgpu_gmc_get_pte_flags(adev, args-&gt;flags);<!----></span>



<br>





		r = amdgpu_vm_bo_replace_map(adev, bo_va, args->va_address,



<span class="line"><!---->		r = amdgpu_vm_bo_replace_map(adev, bo_va, args-&gt;va_address,<!----></span>



<br>





					     args->offset_in_bo, args->map_size, <------



<span class="line"><!---->					     args-&gt;offset_in_bo, args-&gt;map_size, &lt;------<!----></span>



<br>





					     va_flags);



<span class="line"><!---->					     va_flags);<!----></span>



<br>





		break;



<span class="line"><!---->		break;<!----></span>



<br>





	default:



<span class="line"><!---->	default:<!----></span>



<br>





		break;



<span class="line"><!---->		break;<!----></span>



<br>





	}



<span class="line"><!---->	}<!----></span>



<br>





	if (!r && !(args->flags & AMDGPU_VM_DELAY_UPDATE) && !amdgpu_vm_debug)



<span class="line"><!---->	if (!r &amp;&amp; !(args-&gt;flags &amp; AMDGPU_VM_DELAY_UPDATE) &amp;&amp; !amdgpu_vm_debug)<!----></span>



<br>





		amdgpu_gem_va_update_vm(adev, &fpriv->vm, bo_va,



<span class="line"><!---->		amdgpu_gem_va_update_vm(adev, &amp;fpriv-&gt;vm, bo_va,<!----></span>



<br>





					args->operation);



<span class="line"><!---->					args-&gt;operation);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





//skip...



<span class="line"><!---->//skip...<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Use amdgpu_vm_bo_map as example, amdgpu_vm_bo_replace_map has same kind issue:



<span class="line"><!---->Use amdgpu_vm_bo_map as example, amdgpu_vm_bo_replace_map has same kind issue:<!----></span>



<br>





int amdgpu_vm_bo_map(struct amdgpu_device *adev,



<span class="line"><!---->int amdgpu_vm_bo_map(struct amdgpu_device *adev,<!----></span>



<br>





		     struct amdgpu_bo_va *bo_va,



<span class="line"><!---->		     struct amdgpu_bo_va *bo_va,<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->		     uint64_t saddr, uint64_t offset,<!----></span>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->		     uint64_t size, uint64_t flags)<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->//skip...<!----></span>

	/* validate the parameters */



<span class="line"><!---->	/* validate the parameters */<!----></span>



<br>





	if (saddr & ~PAGE_MASK || offset & ~PAGE_MASK ||



<span class="line"><!---->	if (saddr &amp; ~PAGE_MASK || offset &amp; ~PAGE_MASK ||<!----></span>



<br>





	    size == 0 || size & ~PAGE_MASK)



<span class="line"><!---->	    size == 0 || size &amp; ~PAGE_MASK)<!----></span>



<br>





		return -EINVAL;



<span class="line"><!---->		return -EINVAL;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	/* make sure object fit at this offset */



<span class="line"><!---->	/* make sure object fit at this offset */<!----></span>



<br>





	eaddr = saddr + size - 1;



<span class="line"><!---->	eaddr = saddr + size - 1;<!----></span>



<br>





	if (saddr >= eaddr ||



<span class="line"><!---->	if (saddr &gt;= eaddr ||<!----></span>



<br>





	    (bo && offset + size > amdgpu_bo_size(bo)))  <-------- offset and size is from userspace argument, overflow



<span class="line"><!---->	    (bo &amp;&amp; offset + size &gt; amdgpu_bo_size(bo)))  &lt;-------- offset and size is from userspace argument, overflow<!----></span>



<br>





		return -EINVAL;



<span class="line"><!---->		return -EINVAL;<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->        <!----></span>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromiumos/chromiumos/codesearch/+/main:src/third_party/kernel/v5.4/drivers/gpu/drm/amd/amdgpu/amdgpu_gem.c;drc=343d2c1b5bee7fc3a8be64fce342c532a9ed65e4;l=650"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromiumos/chromiumos/codesearch/+/main:src/third_party/kernel/v5.4/drivers/gpu/drm/amd/amdgpu/amdgpu_gem.c;drc=343d2c1b5bee7fc3a8be64fce342c532a9ed65e4;l=650<!----></a>

<br>





After set big offset, the offset will be used later, for example function amdgpu_gem_va_update_vm -> amdgpu_vm_bo_update -> amdgpu_vm_bo_split_mapping.



<span class="line"><!---->After set big offset, the offset will be used later, for example function amdgpu_gem_va_update_vm -&gt; amdgpu_vm_bo_update -&gt; amdgpu_vm_bo_split_mapping.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In function amdgpu_vm_bo_split_mapping:



<span class="line"><!---->In function amdgpu_vm_bo_split_mapping:<!----></span>



<br>





	pfn = mapping->offset >> PAGE_SHIFT;  <------- offset is big value



<span class="line"><!---->	pfn = mapping-&gt;offset &gt;&gt; PAGE_SHIFT;  &lt;------- offset is big value<!----></span>



<br>





	if (nodes) {



<span class="line"><!---->	if (nodes) {<!----></span>



<br>





		while (pfn >= nodes->size) {



<span class="line"><!---->		while (pfn &gt;= nodes-&gt;size) {<!----></span>



<br>





			pfn -= nodes->size;



<span class="line"><!---->			pfn -= nodes-&gt;size;<!----></span>



<br>





			++nodes;       <----------- oob



<span class="line"><!---->			++nodes;       &lt;----------- oob<!----></span>



<br>





		}



<span class="line"><!---->		}<!----></span>



<br>





	}



<span class="line"><!---->	}<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





	do {



<span class="line"><!---->	do {<!----></span>



<br>





		dma_addr_t *dma_addr = NULL;



<span class="line"><!---->		dma_addr_t *dma_addr = NULL;<!----></span>



<br>





		uint64_t max_entries;



<span class="line"><!---->		uint64_t max_entries;<!----></span>



<br>





		uint64_t addr, last;



<span class="line"><!---->		uint64_t addr, last;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





		if (nodes) {



<span class="line"><!---->		if (nodes) {<!----></span>



<br>





			addr = nodes->start << PAGE_SHIFT; <----------- oob



<span class="line"><!---->			addr = nodes-&gt;start &lt;&lt; PAGE_SHIFT; &lt;----------- oob<!----></span>



<br>





			max_entries = (nodes->size - pfn) * <---------- oob



<span class="line"><!---->			max_entries = (nodes-&gt;size - pfn) * &lt;---------- oob<!----></span>



<br>





				AMDGPU_GPU_PAGES_IN_CPU_PAGE;



<span class="line"><!---->				AMDGPU_GPU_PAGES_IN_CPU_PAGE;<!----></span>

		} else {



<span class="line"><!---->		} else {<!----></span>

			addr = 0;

<span class="line"><!---->			max_entries = S64_MAX;<!----></span>

		}



<span class="line"><!---->		}<!----></span>

REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





To demo this issue more convinent, I patched function amdgpu_gem_va_ioctl, modify the args->offset_in_bo to a big value when there is a AMDGPU_VA_OP_MAP or AMDGPU_VA_OP_REPLACE operation ioctl coming,then wait kernel crashes.



<span class="line"><!---->To demo this issue more convinent, I patched function amdgpu_gem_va_ioctl, modify the args-&gt;offset_in_bo to a big value when there is a AMDGPU_VA_OP_MAP or AMDGPU_VA_OP_REPLACE operation ioctl coming,then wait kernel crashes.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





1, build the kernel patch in attachment, flash it



<span class="line"><!---->1, build the kernel patch in attachment, flash it<!----></span>



<br>





2, dmesg -w to wait the kernel crash information, the kernel will crash after about 50 seconds



<span class="line"><!---->2, dmesg -w to wait the kernel crash information, the kernel will crash after about 50 seconds<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>

UPSTREAM: drm/amdgpu: restrict bo mapping within gpu address limits



<span class="line"><!---->UPSTREAM: drm/amdgpu: restrict bo mapping within gpu address limits<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Have strict check on bo mapping since on some systems, such as A+A or



<span class="line"><!---->Have strict check on bo mapping since on some systems, such as A+A or<!----></span>



<br>





hybrid, the cpu might support 5 level paging or can address memory above



<span class="line"><!---->hybrid, the cpu might support 5 level paging or can address memory above<!----></span>



<br>





48 bits but gpu might be limited by hardware to just use 48 bits. In



<span class="line"><!---->48 bits but gpu might be limited by hardware to just use 48 bits. In<!----></span>



<br>





general, this applies to all asics where this limitation can be checked



<span class="line"><!---->general, this applies to all asics where this limitation can be checked<!----></span>



<br>





against their max_pfn range. This restricts the range to map bo within



<span class="line"><!---->against their max_pfn range. This restricts the range to map bo within<!----></span>



<br>





pratical limits of cpu and gpu for shared virtual memory access.



<span class="line"><!---->pratical limits of cpu and gpu for shared virtual memory access.<!----></span>

UPSTREAM: drm/amdgpu: restrict bo mapping within gpu address limits



<span class="line"><!---->UPSTREAM: drm/amdgpu: restrict bo mapping within gpu address limits<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Have strict check on bo mapping since on some systems, such as A+A or



<span class="line"><!---->Have strict check on bo mapping since on some systems, such as A+A or<!----></span>



<br>





hybrid, the cpu might support 5 level paging or can address memory above



<span class="line"><!---->hybrid, the cpu might support 5 level paging or can address memory above<!----></span>



<br>





48 bits but gpu might be limited by hardware to just use 48 bits. In



<span class="line"><!---->48 bits but gpu might be limited by hardware to just use 48 bits. In<!----></span>



<br>





general, this applies to all asics where this limitation can be checked



<span class="line"><!---->general, this applies to all asics where this limitation can be checked<!----></span>



<br>





against their max_pfn range. This restricts the range to map bo within



<span class="line"><!---->against their max_pfn range. This restricts the range to map bo within<!----></span>



<br>





pratical limits of cpu and gpu for shared virtual memory access.



<span class="line"><!---->pratical limits of cpu and gpu for shared virtual memory access.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.<!----></span>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM

        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }

          white-space: nowrap;

          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;

          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }

          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
      </style>

      </div>
